amar yakki fo j ke aala commander general joseph ڈنفورڈ naay kaha hai ke agar Pakistan  aur Afghanistan  naay –apne ilaaqon mein shiddat pasandon par qaboo nah paaya to Al Qaeda  phir se Afghanistan  mein phail jaye gi
Afghanistan  se mukammal inkhilah ke liye sun do hazaar satrah ki hatmi tareekh muqarrar karne ke liye White House ko fouj ne nahi kaha hai, anho n ne yeh baat senate ki armed services committee ko btai

unhon ne kaha ke Afghan  special forces 2017 hamza taq –apne bil botay par dehshat gard giroh Al Qaeda  par dabao nahi daal saken gi
unhon nay﻿ yeh bhi kaha ke agar Afghanistan  aur Pakistan  nay﻿ –apne –apne ilaaqon mein shiddat pasandon par qaboo nah paaya to is baat ka bohat khatrah hai ke Al Qaeda  Afghanistan  mein phir se phail jaye gi aur phir se America  par hamlay karne ke mansoobay banana shuru kar day gi
unhon ne kaha ke sun do hazaar solah mein bhi Afghan  security forces ko –apne tor par ansdadِ dehshat gardi ki karwaiya karne mein mushkilaat ka saamna hoga
general ڈنفورڈ ka mazeed kehna tha ke Afghanistan  se mukammal inkhilah ke liye sun do hazaar satrah ki hatmi tareekh muqarrar karne ke liye White House ko fouj ne nahi kaha tha
unhon ney kaha ke Amrici  aur Afghan  askari qayadat ko Amrici  hakkaam se sun do hazaar satrah ke liye fojion ki tadaad ke baaray mein thora aur mabham rehne ki tawaqqa thi aur is ke sath woh yeh bhi chahtay thay ke dushman ko bain al aqwami forces ke chalay jaanay ka pegham nah diya jaye
jab un se America  ke inkhilah ke mansoobay mein mumkina tabdeeli ke baaray mein poocha gaya to unhon naay kaha ke mojooda schedule ke tehat sun do hazaar solah mein Afghanistan  mein tainaat Amrici  forces mukhtalif ilaqon se kabul muntaqil ho jayen gi jis se ansdadِ dehshat gardi ki karwaiyon mein Amrici  forces ka taawun barri had taq kam ho jaye ga
unhon ney kaha ke agar sun do hazaar solah mein America  ney mazeed madad ki zaroorat ka faisla kya to hakkaam ko is se aik baras pehlay is par ghhor shuru karna ho ga taakay kabul ke ilawa deegar ilaaqon mein larai mein muawnat ke liye Amrici  special operations forces ki dasteyabi ko yakeeni banaya ja sakay

Supreme Court nay﻿ marwaye aeen iqdaam ke hawalay se dair darkhwaston ki samaat 25 augst taq multawi karte hue darkhwast guzaron ki janib se dharnay khatam karne kay khilaaf darkhwast aik baar phir mustard kar di aur kaha hai ke yeh aik intizami maamla hai aur intizami mamlaat ki zimma daar hukoomat hai jabkay adalat nay﻿ darkhwast guzaron ke aatrazat par awaami tehreek se tafseeli jawab chobees ghanton mein talabb kya hai' tehreek insaaf aur awaami tehreek nay﻿ –apne –apne jawabaat Supreme Court mein jama karaye hain
tehreek insaaf nay﻿ kaha hai ke un ke kisi iqdaam se marwaye aeen iqdaam ka koi khatrah nahi
woh pramn hain' pramn rahen ge
container hatakar awaami mushkilaat khatam ki jayen jabkay awaami tehreek nay﻿ –apne jawab mein adalti ikhtiyar ko challenge kya hai aur kaha hai ke adalat ko siyasi mamlaat mein mudakhlat ka ikhtiyar nahi

justice Jawad  s khwaja ne remarks dete hue kaha ke hum paanch judge jaakar logon ko shahrah dastoor se nahi hata satke yeh kaam intizamia ka hai' hukoomat kahan hai woh apna farz kyun ada nahi kar rahi

jummay کوچیف justice ناصرالملک ki sarbarahi mein paanch rukni larger bench nay﻿ case ki samaat ki to Pakistan  tehreek insaaf ki janib se mufasil jabkay awaami tehreek ki janib se ibtidayi jawab daakhil karwaya gaya
Imran  Khan  ki janib se Hamid  Khan  advocate ne tehreeri jawab mein muaqqaf ikhtiyar kya gaya hai ke tehreek insaaf aeen ki baladasti aur qanoon ki hukmarani par yaqeen rakhti hai' karkunaan kisi sarkari imarat mein nah to daakhil hon ge aur nah hi inhen nuqsaan pohanchayen ge
tehreek insaaf yaqeen dilaati hai ke koi aisa iqdaam nahi uthaya jaye ga ke jis se marwaye aeen iqdaam honay ka koi imkaan ho
pi tea aayi waza kardah usoolon ki pabandi kere gi' tamam karkunaan pur aman hain aur pur aman rahen ge' Imran  Khan  qanoon ki hukmarani par yaqeen rakhtay hain' ehtijaj karna har shehri ka haq hai aur yeh dharnay article 4' 9' 15 aur 16 ke tehat dyie jasakte hain
shehrion ki naqal o harkat mein rukawat kntinrz hain inhen hataya jaye' shehrion ko khanay peenay ki ashya faraham nahi honay di jarhin' hukoomat jaan boojh kar khauf ka mahol peda kar rahi hai' adalat se استدعاء ki gayi hai ke shehrion ko un ke bunyadi haqooq se mahroom nah kya jaye
jabkay awaami tehreek ki janib se barrister Ali  Zafar  advocate ne jawab daakhil karate hue kaha ke awaami tehreek aik pur aman jamaat hai
woh insaaf ke liye sarkon par niklee hai
jo bhi rakawaten hain woh hukoomat ki janib se hain
dharnay siyasi maamla hain magar qanooni maamla nahi
awaami tehreek ne muslim league ( noon ) ki terhan Supreme Court par hamla nahi kya
dharnon ki ijazat qanoon deta hai is par justice Saqib  Nisar  ne kaha ke logon ko mushkilaat ka saamna hai
bay shak ehtijaj aap ka aaeni haq hai' kisi aur jagah muntaqil hokar bay shak lambay arsay tak dharna dete rahen hamein koi aitraaz nahi
justice Jawad  s khwaja ne kaha ke adalat ka darwaaza shahrah dastoor par khilta hai hamein mutabadil rastay se aana para
is douran darkhwast guzaron ke wukla nay﻿ adalat se استدعاء ki ke shahrah dastoor se dharnon ko khatam karne ke ehkamaat jari kiye jayen
jis par justice Jawad  s khwaja ney kaha ke aap chahtay hain ke hum paanch judge jayen aur muzahireen ko shahrah dastoor se utthayen

justice Saqib  Nisar  ney kaha ke agar aap bunyadi haqooq ki baat karte hain twas kamtlb hai ke aap aeen ki baat karte hain? justice Saqib  Nisar  ney kaha ke ehtijaj aap ka bunyadi haq hai taham dosaron ke haqooq ka bhi khayaal rakhen, hukoomat bhi zehan mein rakhay ke shahrah dastoor par koi rakawaten nah hon
hukoomat کنیٹنرز htaye aur muzahireen shahrah dastoor khaali kar den
samaat ke douran justice Saqib  Nisar  ne kaha kay ehtijaj sab ka aaeni aur jamhoori haq hai magar dosaron ke haqooq ki khilaaf warzi nah ki jaye, yeh jagah khaali kar ke kisi doosri jagah ka intikhab kya jaye
justice Jawad  s khwaja naay kaha kay sprim court ka darwaaza shahrah dastoor par khilta hai aur ehtijaj ke baais hamein mutabadil rastay se adalat aana para
shahrah dastoor bock karne ki aur nah hi kisi ghair aaeni iqdaam ki himayat karte hain, kisi doosri jagah par aap log –apne mutalibaat ki manzoori taq dharna jari rakhen hamein is par koi aitraaz nahi ho ga
cheif justice nasir almulk naay kaha kay 2 November  2007 ko Aitzaz  Ahsen  naay sprim court mein kaha tha ke marwaye aeen iqdaam honay ja raha hai taham adalat naay un ki darkhwast ki samaat nahi ki aur phir 3 November  ko marwaye aeen iqdaam ho gaya
cheif justice ne kaha ke tehreek insaaf ne wazeh kar diya ke woh marwaye aeen iqdaam ki himayat nahi karti
kntinrz ki wajah se logon ko paidal chalna par raha hai, attorny general jawab den
justice Asif  Saeed  khosa nay﻿ kaha kay ehtijaj krniwalon ke haqooq hain to jo ehtijaj nahi karte un ke bhi haqooq hain, bunyadi haqooq ka maamla hai log maaray ja chuke hain
justice Jawad  s khwaja ne kaha kay hukoomat aeen aur qanoon nafiz kere, koi haail ho raha hai to bitayen
baad azan adalat Uzma ne Pakistan  awaami tehreek se tafseeli jawab talabb karte hue mumkina marwaye aeen iqdaam case ki samaat paiir taq multawi kar di hai

Pakistan  awaami tehreek ke sarbarah allama dr Tahir Al Qaderi  ne kaha hai ke hamein maloom hai ke hukmraanon ke paas koi ikhlaqi qowat nahi hai, yeh bokhlahat ka shikaar hain hukmraanon ke hotay hue kisi ko insaaf nahi mil sakta mojooda hukmaran hitler aur misolini se badter Amir  hain, parliment ke 75 feesad arakeen assembly tax chor hain, corruption ka koi check and balance nahi hai, yahan log apni corruption bachanay ki khatir jamhoriat ka raag alap rahay hain, hukmaran hamaray khilaaf crack down karna chahtay hain to hum wazeh kar dein hum ne sabar o رتحمل ka daman haath se nahi chorra ab hukoomat hamaray suber ko mazeed mat aazamaa_e, aaj jummay ka markazi ijtima bhi d chowk mein hoga, namaz jummay khud prhhaon ga, tehreek insaaf ko bhi jummay mein shirkat ki dawat hai
un khayalat ka izhaar unhon nay﻿ jumaraat ke roz parliment ke samnay inqilab March  ke shurka se khitaab karte hue kya

unhon nay﻿ yeh baat jummay ko zila chnyot aur sargodha mein selaab mutasireen se khitaab karte hue kahi
zila chnyot ki tehseel bhwanh mein wazeer e azam ko selaab se honay walay nuqsanaat aur imdadi sar garmion ke baaray mein breifing di gayi
is mauqa par mutasireen se khitaab karte hue wazeer e azam Mohammad  Nawaz  shareef ne kaha ke mushkil ki is ghari mein sobai aur wifaqi hukoomat mil kar mutasireen ki madad kar rahay hain
unhon ne kaha ke selaab achanak aaya jis se barray pemanay par nuqsaan sun-hwa hai
mutasireen ki janib se' ' Pakistan  zindah bad' ' ke naaron ki goonj mein wazeer e azam ne selaab mutasireen ki himmat, jazbay aur sabrr ke muzahiray ko sarahtay hue kaha ke museebat ki is gharri mein mutasireen ka buland jazba qabil tehseen hai
wazeer e azam naay kaha ke mushkil waqt mein hukoomat mutasireen ke sath hai aur mutasireen ki mushkilaat ke azale ke liye un ke darmain mojood hain, mutasireen dobarah –apne paon par kharray hon ge
wazeer e azam neh kaha ke woh mushkil aur museebat ke waqt selaab zadgaan ka haal poochnay aur un ki musibaton ko kam karne ke liye aaye hain
unhon neh selaab mutasireen ko yaqeen dilaya ke un ke nuqsanaat ko poora kya jaye ga, hukoomat ke paas mehdood wasail ke bawajood is ki awleen tarjeeh selaab se mutasirah afraad ko dobarah –apne paon par khara karna hai, is car kher mein hukoomat peechay nahi rahay gi, mutasireen ke qadam se qadam mila kar chalay gi
wazeer e azam ne kaha ke wifaqi aur sobai hukoomat mil kar mutasireen ke ujre hue gharron ko abad karen gi
wazeer e azam naay kaha ke Pakistan  ki doulat Pakistan  ke awam ki malkiat aur amanat hai, awam ki amanat un par hi kharch ki jaye gi, mushkil ki is gharri mein hukoomat mutasireen ke sath sath ho gi
wazeer e azam ne is azm ka izhaar kiya ke jab tak tamam mutasireen ki abad kaari nahi ho jati woh chain se nahi bathain ge, jin ghareebon ka nuqsaan sun-hwa hai usay poora karne ke liye airee chouti ka zor lagayen ge
wazeer e azam naay kaha ke hukoomat mutasireen ke masail hal karne mein koi kotahi nahi kere gi, mutasireen ko fasal, maal maweshion ka muawza ada kya jaye ga
unhon ne kaha ke woh aindah chand dinon mein imdadi karwaiyon ka jaiza lainay ke liye dobarah dora karen ge
unhon ne chnyot ko aafat zada ilaqa qarar dainay ki bhi Hadayat  jari kee
qabal azeen sargodha mein selaab mutasireen se khitaab karte hue wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef naay kaha ke sargodha ka yeh halqa mujhe bohat Aziz  hai
is halqay se awam nay﻿ mujhe bhi kamyaab karaya tha

wazeer e azam nay﻿ kaha ke wazeer aala Punjab  Shahbaz  shareef Allah  yahan ka dora kar chuke hain aur mein bhi aap ke darmiyan mojood hon
unhon neh kaha ke wazeer aala Punjab  Shahbaz  shareef musalsal selaab mutasireen ke sath hain, woh khud mutasireen ko milnay aur un ki mushkilaat daur karne ke liye mutasirah ilaaqon ka dora kar rahay hain
wazeer e azam Nawaz  shareef ne kaha ke is ilaqay mein selaab se mutasirah gharon ko dobarah taamer karne ke liye madad karen ge, jin ki faslein tabah hui hain Insha  Allah  un ko bhi muawza diya jaye ga
unhon ne kaha ke selaab se sarkain, faslein aur makanaat ko pouncha hai, aik nojawan jaan bahaq sun-hwa
wazeer e azam ne kaha ke inhen mutasireen ki mushkilaat aur dukhoon ka poora ehsas hai, un ki bahaali ka fori tor par kaam shuru ho jaye ga, Allah  se dua karen ke is qoum ko mushkilaat se nijaat ataa farmaiye, hamaray halaat par reham farmaiye, malik ki taraqqi ki tofeq day

yeh kamyabi Afghan  saddar dr Ashraf  ghanni aur cheif executive عبداﷲ عبداﷲ ki Danish  o firasat ke baais mumkin hui jo qaumi mafadaat ko har cheez par foqiat dete hain
is ke nateejay mein Afghanistan  mein aman aur ittehaad ko istehkaam miley ga
unhon ne kaha ke is ahem mourr par saddar Ashraf  ghanni jaisi mazboot qayadat Afghanistan  ke liye khush qismati ka baais hai
tabdeeli aur islahat ke liye un ka agenda dorrs ahmiyat ka haamil hai jo Afghanistan  ke liye maeeshat, salamti aur insani wasail ke istehkaam ki tikon par zor dete hain
–apne dora kabul ka zikar karte hue sartaaj Aziz  ne kaha ke saddar Ashraf  ghanni se mulaqaat se inhen Afghanistan  aur Pakistan  ke darmain khusoosi taluqaat ke vision ka mauqa mila
mein ne Afghanistan  mein aman o istehkaam aur dono mumalik ke darmiyan jame aur paidaar shiraakat daari ki taamer ke liye wazeer e azam Mohammad  Nawaz  shareef ki khwahish ka izhaar kya
sartaaj Aziz  neh kaha ke Afghan  saddar neh bhi un ke sath khittay ko aapas mein milaane ke wazeer e azam ke vision se ittafaq kya jahan tansport rahdaryon se tijarat ko farogh miley aur bijli ke grid stationon aur gas pipe linon se tawanai ki tarseel ho
dayilag ke ihtimaam par pak chaynh institute ki koshisho ki tareef karte hue unhon ne kaha ke woh senetor Mushahid  Hussain  ki dawat ke mashkoor hain aur bain al aqwami conference ke ineqad par pak chaynh institute aur کونراڈ ایڈنیور اسٹیفنگ ki tareef karte hain
unhon ne kaha ke pak China  institute aik fa-aal thnk tank aur public policy ke Laiha  amal ka ahem plate form ban chuka hai
unhon ne kaha ke chain aik aalmi taaqat ki hesiyat se ubhra hai jo mojooda daur ki intahi barri tabdeelion mein se aik hai
chain ki pur aman taraqqi ki policy aur is ka barhta sun-hwa aalmi asar o rasookh Afghanistan  ke sath qareebi raabtey ke liye ahmiyat ka haamil hai

yadrhe ke Dubai  test mein hi jumaraat ko Younis  Khan  ko pehli ining mein 106 runs score kar ke Pakistan  ki janib se tamam 9 test mumalik kay khilaaf centuria bananay walay pehlay khilari ka record bhi –apne naam karne mein kamyaab rahay they, woh ab is test match ki dono ining mein three figr score karne walay Pakistan  ke satwen batsman bhi ban gay hain, is se qabal Hanif  Mohammad  1964, Javed  myandad 1984 Wajahat  واسطی1999, yasir hmid 2003, انضماالحق 2005, aur Mohammad  Yousuf  2006, mein yeh karnaama sar-anjaam day chuke
doosri janib Ahmed  Shahzad  ki century 4 saal baad kisi bhi Pakistani  opener ki janib se Australia  kay khilaaf pehli three فیگراننگز thi, 2000 ke baad sirf 2 centuria Salman  Butt  nay﻿ 2005 aur 2010 mein banayen

31 october ( ae pi pi ) wazeer e azam Mohammad  Nawaz  shareef ne ptrolim masnoaat ki qeematon mein numaya kami ka elaan karte hue kaha hai ke manfi siyasat se qaumi maeeshat ko nuqsaan pouncha hai lekin mojooda hukoomat awam ki behbood aur malik ko taraqqi o khushhali ki shahrah par gamzan karne ke liye prazm hai
unhon ne yeh baat jummay ko yahan wifaqi kabeena ke ijlaas ki sadarat karte hue kahi
wazeer e azam nay﻿ elaan kya ke petrol ki qeemat 103. 62 rupay fi letter se kam kar ke 94. 19 rupay fi letter kar di gayi hai is terhan is mein 9. 43 rupay fi letter ki kami ho gi
diesel ki qeemat 107. 39 rupay se kam kar ke 101. 21 rupay fi letter ho gi aur is mein 6. 18 rupay fi letter kami waqay hui hai
high aaktin ki qeemat 131. 13 se kam kar ke 116. 45 rupay fi letter kar di gayi hai is terhan is mein 14. 68 rupay fi letter kami aayi hai
matti ka tail 95. 68 rupay fi letter se kam kar ke 87. 52 rupay fi letter kar diya gaya hai is terhan is mein 8. 16 rupay fi letter ki kami waqay ho gi
wazeer e azam ne kaha ke is iqdaam se mehengai kam ho gi, ashya ki naqal o hamal ke akhrajaat mein kami ho gi aur aam aadmi ko faida puhanche ga
wazeer e azam nay﻿ kaha ke petroleum masnoaat ki qeematon mein kami ka faida awam ko muntaqil karne mein sobai hakoomaten apna mo-asar kirdaar ada karen
wazeer e azam naay tamam wazraye aala se kaha ke woh awam ke liye tansport ke kirayon ko ptrolim masnoaat ki qeematon mein kami ke mutabiq kam karayen taakay is ka faida khaas tabqa ko nahi balkay awam ko aur malik o qoum ko puhanche
